#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat13;
vec2 u_xlat18;
vec2 u_xlat24;
float u_xlat32;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat18.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat18.xy;
    u_xlat18.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat18.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat4.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat4.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat13.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat6.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxyy * u_xlat6.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat0.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat32 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(u_xlat32);
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat18.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat18.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat4.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);

#else

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat9.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;

    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = abs(u_xlat16_30) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_30 = min(u_xlat16_30, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat5.xy * u_xlat16_7.xx;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(u_xlat16_7.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_16 / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat1.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) * u_xlat16_7.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat1.xzw * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_8.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_8.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_8.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_30) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = log2(u_xlat16_30);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat9.x = exp2(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat10 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_30 = (-u_xlat10) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_30 + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_12 * u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_12 = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_12;
    u_xlat16_12 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_12 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat4.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xzw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat9.xxx + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat28 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat28 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat28 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat28 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat28) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_28 = texture(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat16_28 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + u_xlat28;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = log2(u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat1.xyz = exp2(u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.www + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat4;
    return;
}

SubProgram "gles " {

"// hash: 7499e8f13281dde5

{

    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);

    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat18.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

    u_xlat0.y = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;

    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FurTilling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SketchHalftoneMin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SketchHalftoneMax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SketchColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RampThreshold;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RampSmooth;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat13;
vec2 u_xlat18;
vec2 u_xlat24;
float u_xlat32;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat18.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat18.xy;
    u_xlat18.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat18.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat4.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat4.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat13.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat6.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxyy * u_xlat6.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat0.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat32 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(u_xlat32);
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat18.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat18.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat4.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec4 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
bool u_xlatb9;
float u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump float u_xlat16_12;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat27;
float u_xlat28;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_11.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat9.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_30);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = abs(u_xlat16_30) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_30 = min(u_xlat16_30, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat5.xy * u_xlat16_7.xx;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(u_xlat16_7.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_16 / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat4.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;

#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif

    u_xlatb9 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;

    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat16_30 = abs(u_xlat16_30) + 0.00400000019;

    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);

    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);

    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);

    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_7.x = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(u_xlat16_7.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_16 / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat1.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) * u_xlat16_7.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat1.xzw * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_8.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));

    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_8.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_12 * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_12 = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat6.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxyy * u_xlat6.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat0.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat31 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat18.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat18.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat28 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat28 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat28 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat28 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat28) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat10_28 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat10_28 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + u_xlat28;
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = log2(u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat1.xyz = exp2(u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat10_5.xyz = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat10_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.www + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat4;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = max(u_xlat18.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat18.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat18.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat18.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat18.xy;
    u_xlat18.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat18.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat18.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat4.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat4.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat4.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat13.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat6.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0.xxyy * u_xlat6.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat0.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat18.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat32 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(u_xlat32);
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat18.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat18.x = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat18.xx * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat5.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat5.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat4.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat13.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat13.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat13.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec4 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
bool u_xlatb9;
float u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump float u_xlat16_12;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat27;
float u_xlat28;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_11.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;

vec2 u_xlat23;
vec2 u_xlat24;
float u_xlat27;
float u_xlat28;
float u_xlat29;
float u_xlat31;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat28 = max(u_xlat28, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat28);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat28) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat29 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat29) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat3.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat3.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat3.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat12.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat3.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat3.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat5 = u_xlat23.xxyy * u_xlat5.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat5.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat31 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat23.xy;
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat31 = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat5.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat3.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat12.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat12.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat12.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_29 + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_29 = min(max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_29 = clamp(u_xlat16_29, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat3.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.y * u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_2.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;

    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_8.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_8.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat9.x = exp2(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat12 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat12) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_28 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat4.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xzw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat9.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;

    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat3.xyz);

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat10_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.www + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat4;
    return;
}

{

    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat28 = max(u_xlat28, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat28);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat28) * u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat29) * u_xlat2.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xx * _DigiST1.zw;

    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));

    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat23.xy;
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat31 = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat5.xy;

    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat3.x / u_xlat16_7;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat12.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat12.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;

float u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
mediump float u_xlat16_29;
float u_xlat30;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat9.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);

    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;

    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;

    u_xlat9.x = exp2(u_xlat9.x);

    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;

vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;

float u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;

mediump float u_xlat16_30;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat9.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;

    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);

    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_29 + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_29 = min(max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_29 = clamp(u_xlat16_29, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat3.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xzw * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.y * u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_2.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_8.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_8.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_8.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat9.x = exp2(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat12 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat12) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_28 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat4.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xzw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat9.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat30 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat30 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat30 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_30 = texture(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_30 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + u_xlat30;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = log2(u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.www + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat4;
    return;
}

SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "ENABLE_POST_TONE" "_ATVECTOR_X" "_IFFUR_OFF" "_IFRAMP_OFF" "_SHTYPE_LERP" }
"// hash: a0fb5ccf68d6490d
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	float _Gspeed;

attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;

varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _BumpMap_ST.xy + _BumpMap_ST.zw;

    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat28 = max(u_xlat28, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat28);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat28) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat29 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat29) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);

    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat5.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat30 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * u_xlat23.xy;
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat30 = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat5.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;

    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);

    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;

    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;

    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat3.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat4.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat3.xzw;

    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_2.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;

    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_28 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat4.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xzw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat9.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat30 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat30 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat30 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat10_30 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat10_30 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + u_xlat30;
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat10_5.xyz = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat10_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.www + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat4;
    return;
}

    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat28) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat29 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat29) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat3.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat3.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat3.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat12.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat3.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat3.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat12.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(vec2(_Gspeed, _Gspeed)) * vec2(0.0500000007, -0.0500000007);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat5 = u_xlat23.xxyy * u_xlat5.xyxy + in_TEXCOORD1.xyxy;
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat5.zw + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat24.x = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, -1.0));
    u_xlat24.y = dot(u_xlat23.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat24.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat23.xy = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    u_xlat31 = (-_Gspeed) * 0.318309873 + 1.0;
    u_xlat23.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat23.xy;
    u_xlat6.zw = u_xlat23.xy * vec2(_Maskadjust);
    u_xlat31 = _Gspeed * 0.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat31) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat5.xy * vec2(vec2(_GScale, _GScale));
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat6;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_7 = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat3.x / u_xlat16_7;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_7) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = log2(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_7 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.y = u_xlat16_7 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_8.z = u_xlat16_7 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_TEXCOORD1.x);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat12.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat12.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat12.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}
