void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat9.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat9.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vs_TEXCOORD8.ww;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_7.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(_MatMapMul);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat27 = min(max(u_xlat27, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat27) * u_xlat27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(_RoughNessOffset, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27 + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_29 + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat27 = min(u_xlat27, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_29 = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_29 = min(max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_29 = clamp(u_xlat16_29, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat3.xzw + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_29) + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xzw = u_xlat3.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat3.xzw * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.y * u_xlat16_2.y;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_2.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_8.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_8.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_8.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat9.x = exp2(u_xlat9.x);
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat12 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat12) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat18;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_28 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat4.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xzw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat9.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat9.x = min(u_xlat9.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat30 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat30 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat9.x * u_xlat30 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat30 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat30) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_30 = texture(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_30 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat9.x) + u_xlat30;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat9.x = min(max(u_xlat9.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat9.x = clamp(u_xlat9.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _Gcolor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = log2(u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(_Gcontrast);
    u_xlat3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD1.zw).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;

    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = vec2(0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = min(u_xlat16_1, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_1) + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(0.0500000007, 0.0500000007, 0.0500000007);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_1) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(_DigiScale) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat2.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat2.zzz + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.w = clamp(u_xlat0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0.x = in_TEXCOORD0.y * 2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.z = (-_DigiChange) * 2.0 + u_xlat0.x;

    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_TARGET0;
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
